\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_benchmark-4_2src_2_detector_construction_8cc_source_l02097}02097 \textcolor{comment}{}\textcolor{keywordtype}{void} DetectorConstruction::RodsHexagonalPlacementInHexagonalCore(G4bool overlap, G4int \&Counter\_unplaced, G4int \&N\_fuelrods, G4double cool7V)}

\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_benchmark-4_2src_2_detector_construction_8cc_source_l02100}02100 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_benchmark-4_2src_2_detector_construction_8cc_source_l02101}02101     G4double width=p-\/>dbl\_PolygoneWidth + p-\/>dbl\_rRodsGap;}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_benchmark-4_2src_2_detector_construction_8cc_source_l02102}02102     G4double lateral\_pitch = width * sqrt(3);}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_benchmark-4_2src_2_detector_construction_8cc_source_l02103}02103     G4double diagonal = width / (2 * cos(twopi/12.));   \textcolor{comment}{// Half maximum width of the hexagonal rod}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_benchmark-4_2src_2_detector_construction_8cc_source_l02104}02104     G4int ix\_FromCenter = (int) ((fbreeder\_r/cos(twopi/12.) -\/ diagonal) / lateral\_pitch) + 1;  \textcolor{comment}{// Number of hexagons from the center of the geometry to the inner driver radius}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_benchmark-4_2src_2_detector_construction_8cc_source_l02105}02105     G4double Xmin = fbreeder\_r/cos(twopi/12.) + diagonal, Xmax = (fbreeder\_r + *fFuelAssemblyLength)/cos(twopi/12.)-\/diagonal;}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_benchmark-4_2src_2_detector_construction_8cc_source_l02106}02106     std::vector <G4double> vect\_R\_Theta = \{ix\_FromCenter*lateral\_pitch, 0\}; \textcolor{comment}{// Position in polar coordinates}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_benchmark-4_2src_2_detector_construction_8cc_source_l02107}02107     std::vector <std::vector <G4double>> Vect\_pos;}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_benchmark-4_2src_2_detector_construction_8cc_source_l02108}02108     Vect\_pos.clear();}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_benchmark-4_2src_2_detector_construction_8cc_source_l02109}02109     G4double x=vect\_R\_Theta[0] * cos(vect\_R\_Theta[1]), y; \textcolor{comment}{// Position in cartesian coordinates}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_benchmark-4_2src_2_detector_construction_8cc_source_l02110}02110 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_benchmark-4_2src_2_detector_construction_8cc_source_l02111}02111     \textcolor{keywordflow}{while}(x <= Xmax+1E-\/6 || ((\textcolor{keywordtype}{int})(vect\_R\_Theta[1]*1E6)) < ((\textcolor{keywordtype}{int})(twopi/6.*1E6))) \{   \textcolor{comment}{// Position calculated for 1/6 of the driver zone [0 ; Pi/3]}}
